Packaging SpecificationCREATE TABLE op_packaging_spec (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    sku_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    packaging_spec_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    commercial_unit_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'BOX',    inner_unit_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'SACHET',    inner_unit_per_commercial_unit INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 4,    box_template_id BIGINT NULL,    sachet_template_id BIGINT NULL,    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    effective_from TIMESTAMP NULL,    effective_to TIMESTAMP NULL,    note TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_packaging_spec_code UNIQUE (packaging_spec_code),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_packaging_spec_inner_unit_per_box        CHECK (inner_unit_per_commercial_unit > 0));CREATE INDEX idx_op_packaging_spec_skuON op_packaging_spec(sku_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_packaging_spec_activeON op_packaging_spec(is_active, effective_from, effective_to);Purposecấu hình đóng gói cho SKUkhóa ratio 1 box = 4 sachetsgắn template hộp và template gói2. Packaging OrderCREATE TABLE op_packaging_order (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    packaging_order_no VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,    production_order_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    sku_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    packaging_spec_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    target_box_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL,    target_sachet_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL,    line_id VARCHAR(100) NULL,    order_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'CREATED',    planned_start_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    planned_end_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    created_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    approved_by BIGINT NULL,    approved_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    note TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_packaging_order_no UNIQUE (packaging_order_no),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_packaging_order_production_order        FOREIGN KEY (production_order_id) REFERENCES op_production_order(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_packaging_order_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_packaging_order_packaging_spec        FOREIGN KEY (packaging_spec_id) REFERENCES op_packaging_spec(id),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_packaging_order_target_box_qty        CHECK (target_box_qty > 0),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_packaging_order_target_sachet_qty        CHECK (target_sachet_qty > 0));CREATE INDEX idx_op_packaging_order_batchON op_packaging_order(batch_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_packaging_order_statusON op_packaging_order(order_status);CREATE INDEX idx_op_packaging_order_skuON op_packaging_order(sku_id);Purposeplanning object cho đóng góigắn production order + batch + packaging specđịnh nghĩa sản lượng mục tiêu ở cấp box và sachetStatus valuesCREATEDAPPROVEDREADYIN_PROGRESSSTOPPEDCOMPLETEDCANCELLED3. Packaging JobCREATE TABLE op_packaging_job (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    packaging_job_no VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,    packaging_order_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    line_id VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    machine_id BIGINT NULL,    operator_id BIGINT NULL,    started_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    completed_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    packaging_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'CREATED',    target_box_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL,    packed_box_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    packed_sachet_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    defective_print_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    packaging_loss_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    note TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_packaging_job_no UNIQUE (packaging_job_no),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_packaging_job_order        FOREIGN KEY (packaging_order_id) REFERENCES op_packaging_order(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_packaging_job_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_packaging_job_machine        FOREIGN KEY (machine_id) REFERENCES op_machine(id),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_packaging_job_target_box_qty        CHECK (target_box_qty > 0),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_packaging_job_non_negative_qty        CHECK (            packed_box_qty >= 0 AND            packed_sachet_qty >= 0 AND            defective_print_qty >= 0 AND            packaging_loss_qty >= 0        ));CREATE INDEX idx_op_packaging_job_orderON op_packaging_job(packaging_order_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_packaging_job_batchON op_packaging_job(batch_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_packaging_job_statusON op_packaging_job(packaging_status);CREATE INDEX idx_op_packaging_job_lineON op_packaging_job(line_id, started_at);Purposeexecution object của đóng góigắn line, machine, operator, target qty, packed qtytheo dõi tiến độ lineStatus valuesCREATEDREADYRUNNINGPAUSEDSTOPPEDCOMPLETEDFAILEDCANCELLED4. Packaging Job Unit SummaryCREATE TABLE op_packaging_job_unit (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    packaging_job_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    unit_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    target_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    produced_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    defective_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    rework_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_packaging_job_unit_job        FOREIGN KEY (packaging_job_id) REFERENCES op_packaging_job(id),    CONSTRAINT uq_op_packaging_job_unit_unique        UNIQUE (packaging_job_id, unit_type),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_packaging_job_unit_non_negative        CHECK (            target_qty >= 0 AND            produced_qty >= 0 AND            defective_qty >= 0 AND            rework_qty >= 0        ));CREATE INDEX idx_op_packaging_job_unit_typeON op_packaging_job_unit(unit_type);unit_type valuesBOXSACHETPurposetách rõ số lượng theo cấp hộp và cấp góithuận tiện cho báo cáo line5. Print TemplateCREATE TABLE op_print_template (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    template_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    template_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    template_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    sku_id BIGINT NULL,    is_default BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,    batch_format_rule VARCHAR(255) NULL,    mfg_format_rule VARCHAR(255) NULL,    exp_format_rule VARCHAR(255) NULL,    qr_type VARCHAR(100) NULL,    print_resolution_dpi INT NULL,    print_spec_json TEXT NULL,    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_print_template_code UNIQUE (template_code));CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_template_typeON op_print_template(template_type, is_active);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_template_skuON op_print_template(sku_id);template_type valuesBOXSACHETPurposecấu hình template in hộp / góilưu format batch, NSX, HSD, QR, resolution6. Print DeviceCREATE TABLE op_print_device (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    device_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    device_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    device_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    line_id VARCHAR(100) NULL,    device_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'ACTIVE',    integration_endpoint VARCHAR(500) NULL,    last_heartbeat_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_print_device_code UNIQUE (device_code));CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_device_lineON op_print_device(line_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_device_statusON op_print_device(device_status, is_active);device_status valuesACTIVEIDLERUNNINGPAUSEDERROROFFLINEDISABLEDPurposequản lý máy in tích hợpphục vụ màn hình line đóng gói và heartbeat trạng thái7. Print JobCREATE TABLE op_print_job (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    print_job_no VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,    packaging_job_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    print_device_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    print_template_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    unit_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    requested_print_count INT NOT NULL,    estimated_print_count INT NULL,    successful_print_count INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    failed_print_count INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    started_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    ended_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    print_job_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'CREATED',    created_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    operator_id BIGINT NULL,    note TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_print_job_no UNIQUE (print_job_no),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_job_packaging_job        FOREIGN KEY (packaging_job_id) REFERENCES op_packaging_job(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_job_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_job_device        FOREIGN KEY (print_device_id) REFERENCES op_print_device(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_job_template        FOREIGN KEY (print_template_id) REFERENCES op_print_template(id),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_print_job_requested_count        CHECK (requested_print_count > 0),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_print_job_non_negative_counts        CHECK (            successful_print_count >= 0 AND            failed_print_count >= 0        ));CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_job_packaging_jobON op_print_job(packaging_job_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_job_batchON op_print_job(batch_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_job_statusON op_print_job(print_job_status);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_job_deviceON op_print_job(print_device_id, started_at);unit_type valuesBOXSACHETprint_job_status valuesCREATEDQUEUEDSENTRUNNINGPAUSEDSTOPPEDCOMPLETEDFAILEDCANCELLEDPurposelệnh in chính thức gửi qua integration layerràng buộc batch, device, template, unit type8. Print Job PayloadCREATE TABLE op_print_job_payload (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    print_job_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    sku_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    product_name_short VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    batch_no VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,    mfg_date DATE NOT NULL,    exp_date DATE NOT NULL,    trace_qr_url TEXT NULL,    packaging_template_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    line_id VARCHAR(100) NULL,    operator_id BIGINT NULL,    payload_json TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_print_job_payload_job UNIQUE (print_job_id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_job_payload_job        FOREIGN KEY (print_job_id) REFERENCES op_print_job(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_job_payload_template        FOREIGN KEY (packaging_template_id) REFERENCES op_print_template(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_job_payload_batchON op_print_job_payload(batch_no);Purposelưu payload thực tế gửi máy inhỗ trợ audit, debug integration, replay controlledRequired outbound fieldssku_codeproduct_name_shortbatch_nomfg_dateexp_datetrace_qr_urlpackaging_template_idline_idoperator_id9. Print Execution LogCREATE TABLE op_print_execution_log (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    print_job_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    print_device_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_no VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,    template_used VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    start_time TIMESTAMP NULL,    end_time TIMESTAMP NULL,    estimated_print_count INT NULL,    actual_print_count INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    device_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    error_code VARCHAR(100) NULL,    operator_id BIGINT NULL,    returned_payload_json TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_execution_log_job        FOREIGN KEY (print_job_id) REFERENCES op_print_job(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_execution_log_device        FOREIGN KEY (print_device_id) REFERENCES op_print_device(id),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_print_execution_log_actual_count        CHECK (actual_print_count >= 0));CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_execution_log_jobON op_print_execution_log(print_job_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_execution_log_deviceON op_print_execution_log(print_device_id, start_time);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_execution_log_batchON op_print_execution_log(batch_no);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_execution_log_errorON op_print_execution_log(error_code);Purposelog phản hồi từ thiết bị intruy xuất line, device, operator, batch, errorRequired inbound fields from device/integrationprint_job_iddevice_idbatch_notemplate_usedstart_timeend_timeestimated_print_countdevice_statuserror_code10. Print Error LogCREATE TABLE op_print_error_log (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    print_job_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    packaging_job_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    print_device_id BIGINT NULL,    error_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    error_code VARCHAR(100) NULL,    error_message TEXT NULL,    detected_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,    detected_by BIGINT NULL,    affected_qty INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    resolution_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'OPEN',    resolution_note TEXT NULL,    resolved_by BIGINT NULL,    resolved_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_error_log_job        FOREIGN KEY (print_job_id) REFERENCES op_print_job(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_error_log_packaging_job        FOREIGN KEY (packaging_job_id) REFERENCES op_packaging_job(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_error_log_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_error_log_device        FOREIGN KEY (print_device_id) REFERENCES op_print_device(id),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_print_error_log_affected_qty        CHECK (affected_qty >= 0));CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_error_log_jobON op_print_error_log(print_job_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_error_log_batchON op_print_error_log(batch_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_error_log_statusON op_print_error_log(resolution_status);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_error_log_typeON op_print_error_log(error_type, detected_at);error_type examplesQR_BLURQR_UNREADABLEMISALIGNED_PRINTMISSING_INFOLINE_STOPPEDWRONG_TEMPLATEWRONG_MFG_EXPWRONG_SKUDEVICE_COMMUNICATION_ERRORresolution_status valuesOPENINVESTIGATINGRESOLVEDWAIVEDCLOSEDPurposelưu lỗi in chi tiếtphục vụ kiểm soát line và audit11. Print Stop EventCREATE TABLE op_print_stop_event (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    print_job_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    packaging_job_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    stop_reason_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    stop_reason_note TEXT NULL,    stopped_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,    stopped_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    resume_allowed BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    resumed_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    resumed_by BIGINT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_stop_event_job        FOREIGN KEY (print_job_id) REFERENCES op_print_job(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_stop_event_packaging_job        FOREIGN KEY (packaging_job_id) REFERENCES op_packaging_job(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_print_stop_event_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_stop_event_jobON op_print_stop_event(print_job_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_stop_event_batchON op_print_stop_event(batch_id, stopped_at);CREATE INDEX idx_op_print_stop_event_reasonON op_print_stop_event(stop_reason_code);stop_reason_code examplesBATCH_CHANGEDWRONG_TEMPLATEWRONG_MFGWRONG_EXPWRONG_SKUQR_QUALITY_FAILUREDEVICE_ERRORMANUAL_STOPPurposeghi nhận việc dừng lệnh inhỗ trợ audit khi đổi batch / template / NSX / HSD / SKUVIII.7 Quantity and Packaging SemanticsBox-level controlĐơn vị bán hàng và truy xuất chính là box.Sachet-level controlKhông bắt buộc QR riêng trên từng gói.Gói chỉ cần:batchMFGEXPStandard ratio1 BOX = 4 SACHETSTỷ lệ này được khóa tại op_packaging_spec.inner_unit_per_commercial_unit.VIII.8 Integration BoundaryRequired integration chainProduction Order / Packaging Order        ↓Batch Generator        ↓Printer Integration Service        ↓Printer Device        ↓Print Log Returned        ↓Packaging Control ScreenDatabase implicationApplication/service layer phải thao tác như sau:op_packaging_order / op_packaging_job là upstream business objectsop_print_job_payload là outbound contractop_print_execution_log là inbound integration evidenceop_print_error_log và op_print_stop_event là control/audit objectsForbidden direct actions by printerMáy in hoặc integration adapter không được phép:tạo warehouse receiptsửa batch releasesửa inventory balancetạo QC passVIII.9 Admin Interface RequirementsA. Packaging Line ScreenRequired fields:production_order_nosku_idbatch_codeline_idtarget_box_qtyprinted_box_qtydevice_statusscan_check_statuserror_alertNguồn dữ liệu chính:op_packaging_orderop_packaging_jobop_print_jobop_print_execution_logop_print_error_logB. Print Configuration ScreenRequired fields:box_templatesachet_templateprint_positionbatch_format_rulemfg_exp_ruleqr_typeprint_resolutionNguồn dữ liệu chính:op_print_templateop_packaging_specC. Print Log ScreenRequired fields:timelineprinter_devicebatchprint_counterroroperatorNguồn dữ liệu chính:op_print_execution_logop_print_error_logop_print_deviceVIII.10 Mobile / Line Interface RequirementsWorkflow vận hành line phải hỗ trợ:open packaging jobselect current batchbind printer devicestart print jobpause print jobstop print jobrecord print defectresume print jobcomplete packaging jobRequired fields:packaging_job_nobatch_codedevice_codetemplate_codeoperator_idrequested_print_countactual_print_counterror_codestop_reason_codeevent_timestampVIII.11 Dev Implementation TasksThứ mismatchRecommended verification query:SELECT pj.print_job_no, pjp.batch_no, b.batch_codeFROM op_print_job pjJOIN op_print_job_payload pjp ON pjp.print_job_id = pj.idLEFT JOIN op_batch b ON stop event with:stop_reason_code = WRONG_TEMPLATEstopped_by = operator_idstopped_at = timestampExpected result:validresume fields initially nullVIII.13 Completion CriteriaModule = op_packaging_jobpackaging level summary = op_packaging_job_unittemplate control = op_print_templatedevice control = op_print_deviceoutbound print contract = op_print_job_payloadinbound print evidence = op_print_execution_logprint quality/error audit = op_print_error_logstop control = op_print_stop_eventKẾT THÚCIX. QC & BATCH RELEASE – DATABASE SCHEMATRIỂN KHAIIX.1 Functional ObjectiveModule này triển khai kiểm tra chất lượng batch và phê duyệt batch release trước khi batch được phép trở thành tồn kho sẵn sàng bán.QC là quality control boundary giữa:· manufacturing / packaging· warehouse receipt· inventory availabilityModule phải bảo đảm các mục tiêu sau:· tiếp nhận batch sau sản xuất / đóng gói· chuyển batch sang trạng thái chờ QC· thực hiện kiểm tra chất lượng theo checklist· ghi nhận kết quả QC· lượng hóa:· accepted_qty· rejected_qty· rework_qty· hold_qty nếu có· quyết định disposition:· accepted· rejected· hold· rework· chỉ batch đạt QC và được release mới được nhập kho thành phẩm· toàn bộ thay đổi trạng thái batch phải có audit trailIX.2 Core Transaction FlowCreated / In-Process / Packaged Batch      ↓QC Pending      ↓QC Inspection      ↓QC Result Recording      ↓Disposition Decision      ↓Batch Release Approval      ↓Eligible for Warehouse ReceiptIX.3 Core EntitiesModule này tạo các bảng chính sau:· op_qc_checklist_template· op_qc_checklist_item· op_qc_inspection· op_qc_inspection_item· op_qc_scan_verification· op_qc_media· op_batch_disposition· op_batch_release· op_batch_state_transition_logIX.4 Data Model RulesRule 1 — QC is mandatory before warehouse receiptBatch không được nhập kho nếu chưa có:· QC inspection hợp lệ· QC result accepted· batch release approvedRule 2 — QC result and release decision are different objectsQC result accepted không đồng nghĩa RELEASED.· QC xác định batch đạt chất lượng· QA / authorized approver xác định batch được releaseRule 3 — Batch lifecycle only covers manufacturing → QC → releaseop_batch.batch_status chỉ được dùng cho vòng đời:· tạo batch· đang sản xuất / hoàn thiện· chờ QC· QC pass / hold / reject· released / blocked / closedKhông được dùng op_batch.batch_status để chứa trạng thái downstream của:· warehouse receipt· allocation· shipment· recall executionRule 4 — Warehouse / inventory / shipment / recall dùng state riêngCác trạng thái sau thuộc module downstream, không phải batch lifecycle state:· WAREHOUSE_RECEIVED· ALLOCATED· SHIPPED· QUARANTINED· RECALLED· RECALL_HOLDChúng phải được quản lý ở:· warehouse receipt· inventory movement / inventory balance· shipment allocation· incident / recall tablesRule 5 — Batch state transition must be explicitKhông suy diễn ngầm trạng thái batch từ:· số lượng· log in· inventory movement· shipment eventRule 6 — Batch state must be auditedMọi thay đổi op_batch.batch_status phải:1. đi qua service layer2. validate transition hợp lệ3. ghi vào op_batch_state_transition_log4. ghi actor + timestamp + reason nếu cóIX.5 Canonical Batch Lifecycle LockCanonical batch states của op_batch.batch_status:· CREATED· IN_PROCESS· PACKAGED· QC_PENDING· QC_PASS· QC_HOLD· QC_REJECT· RELEASED· BLOCKED· CLOSEDCanonical transitions:· CREATED → IN_PROCESS· IN_PROCESS → PACKAGED· PACKAGED → QC_PENDING· QC_PENDING → QC_PASS· QC_PENDING → QC_HOLD· QC_PENDING → QC_REJECT· QC_HOLD → QC_PASS· QC_HOLD → QC_REJECT· QC_PASS → RELEASED· QC_REJECT → BLOCKED· RELEASED → CLOSED· BLOCKED → CLOSEDMandatory system rules:1. batch_status = RELEASED là điều kiện batch đủ chuẩn đi sang warehouse receipt2. batch_status = QC_HOLD, QC_REJECT, BLOCKED không được đi vào warehouse receipt3. allocation / shipment / recall không được update vào op_batch.batch_status4. inventory / shipment / recall phải đọc batch_id làm reference key, không chiếm ownership lifecycle của batchIX.5.1 Mapping Rule Between QC Result and Batch StatusĐể tránh lệch vocabulary:· op_qc_inspection.qc_result = ACCEPTED  → op_batch.batch_status = QC_PASS· op_qc_inspection.qc_result = HOLD      → op_batch.batch_status = QC_HOLD· op_qc_inspection.qc_result = REJECTED  → op_batch.batch_status = QC_REJECT· op_qc_inspection.qc_result = REWORK    → giữ ở QC_HOLD hoặc disposition riêng theo service rule· RELEASED chỉ được set bởi BatchReleaseService, không được set trực tiếp từ QC inspectionIX.6 Database Schema1. QC Checklist TemplateCREATE TABLE op_qc_checklist_template (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    template_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    template_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    sku_id BIGINT NULL,    qc_stage VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'FINISHED_GOODS',    version_no INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    effective_from TIMESTAMP NULL,    effective_to TIMESTAMP NULL,    note TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_qc_checklist_template_code UNIQUE (template_code, version_no));CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_checklist_template_skuON op_qc_checklist_template(sku_id, is_active);CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_checklist_template_stageON op_qc_checklist_template(qc_stage, is_active);Purposechecklist QC theo SKUversion hóa rule QCqc_stage valuesINCOMINGIN_PROCESSFINISHED_GOODS2. QC Checklist ItemCREATE TABLE op_qc_checklist_item (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    checklist_template_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    item_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    item_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    item_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    is_required BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    sort_order INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    acceptance_rule TEXT NULL,    note TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_checklist_item_template        FOREIGN KEY (checklist_template_id) REFERENCES op_qc_checklist_template(id),    CONSTRAINT uq_op_qc_checklist_item_unique        UNIQUE (checklist_template_id, item_code));CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_checklist_item_templateON op_qc_checklist_item(checklist_template_id, sort_order);item_type examplesVISUALPACKAGINGPRINTQR_SCANWEIGHTSENSORYCHECKBOXNUMERICTEXTPurposedanh mục tiêu chí QC trong từng checklist3. QC InspectionCREATE TABLE op_qc_inspection (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    inspection_no VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    checklist_template_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    production_order_id BIGINT NULL,    packaging_job_id BIGINT NULL,    inspected_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    inspected_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,    qc_result VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    accepted_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    rejected_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    rework_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    hold_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    defect_summary TEXT NULL,    recommendation VARCHAR(50) NULL,    inspection_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'COMPLETED',    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_qc_inspection_no UNIQUE (inspection_no),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_inspection_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_inspection_template        FOREIGN KEY (checklist_template_id) REFERENCES op_qc_checklist_template(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_inspection_production_order        FOREIGN KEY (production_order_id) REFERENCES op_production_order(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_inspection_packaging_job        FOREIGN KEY (packaging_job_id) REFERENCES op_packaging_job(id),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_qc_inspection_qty_non_negative        CHECK (            accepted_qty >= 0 AND            rejected_qty >= 0 AND            rework_qty >= 0 AND            hold_qty >= 0        ));CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_inspection_batchON op_qc_inspection(batch_id, inspected_at);CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_inspection_resultON op_qc_inspection(qc_result);CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_inspection_inspected_atON op_qc_inspection(inspected_at);qc_result valuesACCEPTEDREJECTEDHOLDREWORKPENDINGrecommendation valuesRELEASEREJECTHOLDREWORKQUARANTINESCRAPPurposebản ghi kiểm batch chínhlưu kết quả QC, số lượng accepted/rejected/rework/hold4. QC Inspection Item ResultCREATE TABLE op_qc_inspection_item (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    qc_inspection_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    checklist_item_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    result_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    result_value_text TEXT NULL,    result_value_num NUMERIC(18,3) NULL,    defect_code VARCHAR(100) NULL,    defect_note TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_inspection_item_inspection        FOREIGN KEY (qc_inspection_id) REFERENCES op_qc_inspection(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_inspection_item_checklist_item        FOREIGN KEY (checklist_item_id) REFERENCES op_qc_checklist_item(id),    CONSTRAINT uq_op_qc_inspection_item_unique        UNIQUE (qc_inspection_id, checklist_item_id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_inspection_item_inspectionON op_qc_inspection_item(qc_inspection_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_inspection_item_statusON op_qc_inspection_item(result_status);result_status valuesPASSFAILHOLDNAPurposelưu kết quả chi tiết từng tiêu chí QC5. QC Scan VerificationCREATE TABLE op_qc_scan_verification (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    qc_inspection_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    scan_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    scan_result VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    scanned_code TEXT NULL,    scanner_device_id VARCHAR(100) NULL,    scanned_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,    scanned_by BIGINT NULL,    failure_reason TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_scan_verification_inspection        FOREIGN KEY (qc_inspection_id) REFERENCES op_qc_inspection(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_scan_verification_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_scan_verification_inspectionON op_qc_scan_verification(qc_inspection_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_scan_verification_batchON op_qc_scan_verification(batch_id, scanned_at);scan_type valuesQRBARCODETEXT_CODEscan_result valuesREADABLEUNREADABLEMISMATCHFAILEDPurposexác thực QR đọc được / mã in đúng6. QC Media EvidenceCREATE TABLE op_qc_media (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    qc_inspection_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    media_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    media_url TEXT NOT NULL,    uploaded_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    uploaded_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,    caption TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_media_inspection        FOREIGN KEY (qc_inspection_id) REFERENCES op_qc_inspection(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_qc_media_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_media_inspectionON op_qc_media(qc_inspection_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_qc_media_batchON op_qc_media(batch_id);Purposelưu ảnh mẫu, bằng chứng lỗi, bằng chứng QC7. Batch DispositionCREATE TABLE op_batch_disposition (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    qc_inspection_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    disposition_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    disposition_reason_code VARCHAR(100) NULL,    disposition_note TEXT NULL,    effective_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,    decided_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_batch_disposition_inspection UNIQUE (qc_inspection_id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_batch_disposition_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_batch_disposition_inspection        FOREIGN KEY (qc_inspection_id) REFERENCES op_qc_inspection(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_batch_disposition_batchON op_batch_disposition(batch_id, effective_at);CREATE INDEX idx_op_batch_disposition_typeON op_batch_disposition(disposition_type);disposition_type valuesACCEPTEDREJECTEDHOLDREWORKQUARANTINESCRAPPurposequyết định nghiệp vụ sau QCtách khỏi inspection raw result8. Batch ReleaseCREATE TABLE op_batch_release (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    release_no VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    qc_inspection_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    release_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    approved_by BIGINT NULL,    approved_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    qa_lead_required BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,    qa_lead_approved_by BIGINT NULL,    qa_lead_approved_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    release_note TEXT NULL,    created_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_batch_release_no UNIQUE (release_no),    CONSTRAINT uq_op_batch_release_batch UNIQUE (batch_id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_batch_release_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_batch_release_inspection        FOREIGN KEY (qc_inspection_id) REFERENCES op_qc_inspection(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_batch_release_statusON op_batch_release(release_status);CREATE INDEX idx_op_batch_release_approved_atON op_batch_release(approved_at);release_status valuesPENDINGRELEASEDHOLDREJECTEDCANCELLEDPurposequyết định release chính thứccó thể yêu cầu QA lead phê duyệt9. Batch State Transition LogCREATE TABLE op_batch_state_transition_log (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    from_state VARCHAR(50) NULL,    to_state VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    transition_reason_code VARCHAR(100) NULL,    transition_note TEXT NULL,    triggered_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    triggered_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,    source_module VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    source_entity_type VARCHAR(100) NULL,    source_entity_id BIGINT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_batch_state_transition_log_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_batch_state_transition_log_batchON op_batch_state_transition_log(batch_id, triggered_at);CREATE INDEX idx_op_batch_state_transition_log_to_stateON op_batch_state_transition_log(to_state);CREATE INDEX idx_op_batch_state_transition_log_sourceON op_batch_state_transition_log(source_module, source_entity_type);Purposeaudit log bắt buộc cho state machinekhông dùng bảng này để thay current statecurrent state vẫn nằm tại op_batch.batch_statusIX.7 Required State Update Rules on op_batchCurrent state holderop_batch.batch_status là trạng thái hiện tại của batch.Update policyMọi thay đổi op_batch.batch_status chỉ được thực hiện thông qua service layer, đồng thời bắt buộc:1. insert vào op_batch_state_transition_log2. validate transition hợp lệ3. kiểm tra quyền actor4. kiểm tra source entity liên quan5. không được dùng downstream state để ghi đè batch lifecycleCanonical batch states· CREATED· IN_PROCESS· PACKAGED· QC_PENDING· QC_PASS· QC_HOLD· QC_REJECT· RELEASED· BLOCKED· CLOSEDValid transitionsCREATED → IN_PROCESSIN_PROCESS → PACKAGEDPACKAGED → QC_PENDINGQC_PENDING → QC_PASSQC_PENDING → QC_HOLDQC_PENDING → QC_REJECTQC_HOLD → QC_PASSQC_HOLD → QC_REJECTQC_PASS → RELEASEDQC_REJECT → BLOCKEDRELEASED → CLOSEDBLOCKED → CLOSEDHard forbidden transitionsKhông được ghi các trạng thái sau vào op_batch.batch_status:· WAREHOUSE_RECEIVED· ALLOCATED· SHIPPED· QUARANTINED· RECALL_HOLD· RECALLEDCác trạng thái trên thuộc ownership của module downstream:· warehouse receipt· inventory movement / inventory balance· shipment allocation· incident / recallIX.8 Quantity Reconciliation Ruleop_qc_inspection và op_batch_quantity_summary phải đồng bộ theo nguyên tắc reconciliation như sau:A. Upstream reference quantity· produced_qty là số lượng đầu ra từ manufacturing· giá trị này thuộc ownership của manufacturing execution / batch quantity summaryB. QC decision quantities· accepted_qty từ QC = phần đạt chất lượng· rejected_qty từ QC = phần lỗi· rework_qty từ QC = phần cần tái xử lý· hold_qty từ QC = phần tạm giữC. Downstream warehouse quantity· warehouse_receipt_qty chỉ được cập nhật tại module warehouse receipt· QC module không được cập nhật trực tiếp warehouse_receipt_qtyReconciliation rules1. accepted_qty + rejected_qty + rework_qty + hold_qty không được vượt produced_qty2. warehouse_receipt_qty phải <= accepted_qty3. warehouse_receipt_qty chỉ bằng accepted_qty khi:   · batch đã RELEASED   · warehouse đã nhận đủ   · không còn hold / quarantine / staged receipt4. không ép accepted_qty = warehouse_receipt_qty trong cùng transaction QC5. quantity reconciliation chỉ là rule đối chiếu, không làm đổi ownership dữ liệu giữa QC và WarehouseTypical caseaccepted_qty = warehouse_receipt_qtyValid exceptions· staged receipt· quarantine pending· partial warehouse receipt· hold portion chưa nhập kho· accepted portion chia nhiều lần nhập khoIX.9 Admin Interface RequirementsA. QC DashboardRequired metrics:batches_pending_qcbatches_acceptedbatches_on_holdbatches_rejecteddefect_rate_by_linedefect_rate_by_dayacceptance_raterejection_rateNguồn dữ liệu:op_qc_inspectionop_batchop_batch_dispositionop_batch_releaseB. Batch QC ScreenRequired sections:batch informationproduction quantitysample imagesqc checklistqr scan resultsdefect notesaccepted_qtyrejected_qtyrework suggestionhold / quarantine suggestionNguồn dữ liệu:op_batchop_batch_quantity_summaryop_qc_checklist_templateop_qc_inspectionop_qc_inspection_itemop_qc_scan_verificationop_qc_mediaC. Batch Release ScreenRequired actions:confirm_releaseconfirm_holdconfirm_rejectqa_lead_approval_if_requiredNguồn dữ liệu:op_batch_releaseop_batch_dispositionop_batch_state_transition_logIX.10 Mobile / QC Interface RequirementsWorkflow vận hành QC trên mobile / tablet:open batchview sample / batch infoexecute qc checklistscan qrcapture evidenceenter accepted / rejected / rework qtysubmit qc resultrequest release / hold / rejectRequired fields:batch_codeinspection_nochecklist_templatechecklist item resultsscan resultaccepted_qtyrejected_qtyrework_qtydefect_notemedia evidenceinspected_byinspected_atIX.11 Dev Implementation TasksThứ tự migration đề xuất:051_create_op_qc_checklist_template.sql052_create_op_qc_checklist_item.sql053_create_op_qc_inspection.sql054_create_op_qc_inspection_item.sql055_create_op_qc_scan_verification.sql056_create_op_qc_media.sql057_create_op_batch_disposition.sql058_create_op_batch_release.sql059_create_op_batch_state_transition_log.sqlFolder:/database/operational/04_qc_release/IX.12 Required Service-Layer ControlCác rule sau không chỉ khóa ở DB mà còn phải khóa ở service layer.Service: QCInspectionServiceResponsibilities:· tạo inspection· ghi checklist item results· lưu media evidence· lưu scan verification· validate quantity split với produced_qty / batch quantity summary· map qc_result sang batch status:  · ACCEPTED  → QC_PASS  · HOLD      → QC_HOLD  · REJECTED  → QC_REJECT  · REWORK    → QC_HOLD hoặc disposition riêng theo service rule· ghi op_batch_state_transition_log khi cập nhật batch status ở pha QCService: BatchDispositionServiceResponsibilities:· tạo disposition decision· lưu disposition_type· lưu reason code / note· validate consistency với qc_resultService: BatchReleaseServiceResponsibilities:· tạo release decision· validate actor authority· validate batch current state· chỉ cho phép RELEASED khi batch_status hiện tại = QC_PASS· set op_batch.batch_status = RELEASED hoặc BLOCKED theo rule· ghi op_batch_state_transition_logForbidden behavior· không update trực tiếp op_batch.batch_status từ UI· không cho warehouse receipt nếu batch chưa RELEASED· không ghi downstream state vào op_batch.batch_status· không cho module warehouse / inventory / shipment tự sửa batch lifecycleIX.13 Validation TestsTest 1 — Batch enters QC pendingUpdate batch state:PACKAGED → QC_PENDINGExpected result:· valid· state transition log insertedTest 2 — QC accepted maps to QC_PASS, not auto-releaseCreate inspection:qc_result = ACCEPTEDExpected result:· op_qc_inspection valid· op_batch.batch_status = QC_PASS· chưa có warehouse receipt· chưa allocate order nếu chưa có op_batch_release.release_status = RELEASEDTest 3 — Rejected batch cannot be releasedCreate:qc_result = REJECTEDdisposition_type = REJECTEDAttempt batch release:release_status = RELEASEDExpected result:· bị chặn ở service rule· batch_status không được chuyển sang RELEASEDTest 4 — Hold batch excluded from downstream availabilitySet state:QC_HOLDExpected result:· batch không đủ điều kiện cho warehouse receipt· batch không xuất hiện trong danh sách available cho downstream allocationTest 5 — Transition audit must existSau mỗi thay đổi trạng thái, chạy:SELECT *FROM op_batch_state_transition_logWHERE batch_id = :batch_idORDER BY triggered_at;Expected result:· đầy đủ mọi transition· không thiếu recordTest 6 — Quantity split validationInsert inspection:accepted_qty = 1900rejected_qty = 100rework_qty = 0hold_qty = 0Expected result:· valid nếu produced_qty >= 2000· không ép accepted_qty = warehouse_receipt_qty trong cùng transaction QC· warehouse_receipt_qty vẫn do module warehouse cập nhật ở bước sauIX.14 Completion CriteriaModule QC & Batch Release được xem là khóa xong khi:có checklist template theo SKUcó inspection record theo batchcó inspection item resultscó QR scan verificationcó media evidencecó disposition decisioncó release decisioncó batch state transition audit logbatch chưa release không thể nhập kho• batch QC_HOLD / QC_REJECT / BLOCKED không đủ điều kiện đi vào warehouse receipt và downstream allocationIX.15 Technical Lock ResultPhần này khóa xong các nội dung kỹ thuật sau:QC checklist model = op_qc_checklist_template + op_qc_checklist_itemQC transaction object = op_qc_inspectionQC detail result = op_qc_inspection_itemQR verification evidence = op_qc_scan_verificationQC media evidence = op_qc_mediapost-QC business decision = op_batch_dispositionrelease approval object = op_batch_releasebatch lifecycle audit = op_batch_state_transition_logKẾT THÚCTRIỂN KHAIX. WAREHOUSE RECEIPT & INVENTORY CONTROL – DATABASE SCHEMAModule này triển khai nhập kho thành phẩm và kiểm soát tồn kho theo batch.Đây là boundary bắt buộc giữa:QC accepted / batch releasedinventory activationwarehouse stock availabilitydownstream allocation / shipmentX.1 Functional ObjectiveModule phải bảo đảm các mục tiêu sau:chỉ batch đủ điều kiện mới được nhập khonhập kho được ghi nhận bằng warehouse receipt transaction hợp lệtồn kho chỉ tăng sau khi warehouse receipt được xác nhậntồn kho được quản lý theo:batchwarehouselocationstock statusnếu accepted_qty khác warehouse_receipt_qty thì bắt buộc có lý dotoàn bộ biến động tồn kho phải đi qua inventory ledgerX.2 Core Transaction FlowBatch Released      ↓Ready for Receipt      ↓Warehouse Receipt Draft      ↓Quantity Validation      ↓Receipt Confirmation      ↓Inventory Ledger Entry      ↓Inventory Balance Update      ↓Available Inventory by Batch / Warehouse / LocationX.3 Core Data Model RulesRule 1 — Production completion does not create inventorySản xuất xong không tạo tồn kho.Tồn kho chỉ tăng khi:batch đã QC acceptedbatch đã releasedwarehouse receipt đã confirmedRule 2 — Warehouse receipt is the inventory activation pointwarehouse_receipt là transaction kích hoạt tồn kho.Rule 3 — Inventory is lot/batch/location basedTồn kho phải đọc được theo:batchwarehouselocationstock statusRule 4 — Receipt variance requires reasonNếu:accepted_qty <> warehouse_receipt_qtythì phải có:variance_reason_codevariance_noteactortimestampRule 5 — Ledger is append-only movement historyinventory_ledger là lịch sử biến động.Không sửa ledger để “chỉnh số”.Điều chỉnh phải tạo movement mới.X.4 Core EntitiesModule này tạo các bảng chính sau:op_warehouseop_warehouse_locationop_warehouse_receiptop_warehouse_receipt_itemop_inventory_lot_balanceop_inventory_ledgerop_inventory_adjustment_reasonop_inventory_alert_ruleX.5 Database Schema1. Warehouse MasterCREATE TABLE op_warehouse (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    warehouse_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    warehouse_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    warehouse_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'FINISHED_GOODS',    address TEXT NULL,    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_warehouse_code UNIQUE (warehouse_code));CREATE INDEX idx_op_warehouse_typeON op_warehouse(warehouse_type, is_active);warehouse_type valuesRAW_MATERIALWIPFINISHED_GOODSQUARANTINERETURNSCRAPPurposedanh mục khodùng cho receipt, tồn kho, cảnh báo, recall2. Warehouse Location MasterCREATE TABLE op_warehouse_location (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    warehouse_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    location_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    location_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    location_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'STORAGE',    is_pickable BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_warehouse_location_unique UNIQUE (warehouse_id, location_code),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_warehouse_location_warehouse        FOREIGN KEY (warehouse_id) REFERENCES op_warehouse(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_warehouse_location_warehouseON op_warehouse_location(warehouse_id, is_active);CREATE INDEX idx_op_warehouse_location_pickableON op_warehouse_location(is_pickable, is_active);location_type valuesRECEIVINGSTORAGEQUARANTINESTAGINGPICKINGBLOCKEDSCRAPPurposevị trí trong khophục vụ tồn kho theo location3. Inventory Adjustment Reason ReferenceCREATE TABLE op_inventory_adjustment_reason (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    reason_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    reason_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    reason_group VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    sort_order INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_inventory_adjustment_reason_code UNIQUE (reason_code));CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_adjustment_reason_groupON op_inventory_adjustment_reason(reason_group, is_active);reason_group valuesRECEIPT_VARIANCEDAMAGEPRINT_ERRORPACKAGING_ERRORDATE_ERRORWEIGHT_ERRORREWORKSCRAPQUARANTINEOTHERSeed examplesPACKAGING_DEFECTQR_PRINT_ERRORWRONG_DATESEAL_OPENWEIGHT_MISMATCHBROKEN_PRODUCTSENSORY_DEFECTBOX_TORNPACK_RATIO_ERRORPENDING_REWORKSCRAP_DISPOSALQUARANTINE_PENDINGPurposechuẩn hóa lý do chênh lệch / điều chỉnh tồn kho4. Warehouse Receipt HeaderCREATE TABLE op_warehouse_receipt (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    receipt_no VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,    warehouse_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    location_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    receipt_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'FINISHED_GOODS_RECEIPT',    receipt_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'DRAFT',    receipt_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    created_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    confirmed_by BIGINT NULL,    confirmed_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    note TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    is_deleted BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,    deleted_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_warehouse_receipt_no UNIQUE (receipt_no),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_warehouse_receipt_warehouse        FOREIGN KEY (warehouse_id) REFERENCES op_warehouse(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_warehouse_receipt_location        FOREIGN KEY (location_id) REFERENCES op_warehouse_location(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_warehouse_receipt_statusON op_warehouse_receipt(receipt_status);CREATE INDEX idx_op_warehouse_receipt_dateON op_warehouse_receipt(receipt_at);CREATE INDEX idx_op_warehouse_receipt_warehouseON op_warehouse_receipt(warehouse_id, location_id);receipt_status valuesDRAFTPENDING_CONFIRMCONFIRMEDCANCELLEDPurposephiếu nhập kho thành phẩmheader transaction của receipt5. Warehouse Receipt ItemCREATE TABLE op_warehouse_receipt_item (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    warehouse_receipt_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    sku_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    accepted_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL,    warehouse_receipt_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL,    stock_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'ON_HAND',    variance_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    variance_reason_code VARCHAR(100) NULL,    variance_note TEXT NULL,    scanned_batch_code VARCHAR(120) NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_warehouse_receipt_item_receipt        FOREIGN KEY (warehouse_receipt_id) REFERENCES op_warehouse_receipt(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_warehouse_receipt_item_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_warehouse_receipt_item_variance_reason        FOREIGN KEY (variance_reason_code) REFERENCES op_inventory_adjustment_reason(reason_code),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_warehouse_receipt_item_non_negative        CHECK (            accepted_qty >= 0 AND            warehouse_receipt_qty >= 0 AND            variance_qty >= 0        ),    CONSTRAINT uq_op_warehouse_receipt_item_batch UNIQUE (warehouse_receipt_id, batch_id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_warehouse_receipt_item_batchON op_warehouse_receipt_item(batch_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_warehouse_receipt_item_skuON op_warehouse_receipt_item(sku_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_warehouse_receipt_item_stock_statusON op_warehouse_receipt_item(stock_status);stock_status valuesON_HANDAVAILABLEQUARANTINEDHOLDBLOCKEDREWORKSCRAPPurposechi tiết batch nhập kholưu accepted_qty, receipt_qty, variance_qtybắt buộc lưu lý do khi có chênh lệch6. Inventory Lot BalanceCREATE TABLE op_inventory_lot_balance (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    warehouse_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    location_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    sku_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    stock_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'ON_HAND',    on_hand_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    allocated_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    available_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    quarantined_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    damaged_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    recalled_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    nearest_exp_date DATE NULL,    last_movement_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_inventory_lot_balance_unique        UNIQUE (warehouse_id, location_id, batch_id, stock_status),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_lot_balance_warehouse        FOREIGN KEY (warehouse_id) REFERENCES op_warehouse(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_lot_balance_location        FOREIGN KEY (location_id) REFERENCES op_warehouse_location(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_lot_balance_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_inventory_lot_balance_non_negative        CHECK (            on_hand_qty >= 0 AND            allocated_qty >= 0 AND            available_qty >= 0 AND            quarantined_qty >= 0 AND            damaged_qty >= 0 AND            recalled_qty >= 0        ));CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_lot_balance_batchON op_inventory_lot_balance(batch_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_lot_balance_skuON op_inventory_lot_balance(sku_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_lot_balance_expON op_inventory_lot_balance(nearest_exp_date);CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_lot_balance_lookupON op_inventory_lot_balance(warehouse_id, location_id, stock_status, available_qty);Purposetrạng thái tồn kho hiện tại theo batch / kho / vị trí / trạng tháibảng đọc nhanh cho dashboard, picking, recall, near-expiry alertRuleBảng này là current-state projection, không phải lịch sử.7. Inventory LedgerCREATE TABLE op_inventory_ledger (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    ledger_no VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,    transaction_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    source_document_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    source_document_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    sku_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    warehouse_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    location_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    stock_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    qty_in NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    qty_out NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    balance_after NUMERIC(18,3) NULL,    reason_code VARCHAR(100) NULL,    reason_note TEXT NULL,    transaction_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,    performed_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_inventory_ledger_no UNIQUE (ledger_no),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_ledger_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_ledger_warehouse        FOREIGN KEY (warehouse_id) REFERENCES op_warehouse(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_ledger_location        FOREIGN KEY (location_id) REFERENCES op_warehouse_location(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_ledger_reason        FOREIGN KEY (reason_code) REFERENCES op_inventory_adjustment_reason(reason_code),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_inventory_ledger_non_negative        CHECK (            qty_in >= 0 AND            qty_out >= 0        ),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_inventory_ledger_direction        CHECK (            NOT (qty_in > 0 AND qty_out > 0)        ));CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_ledger_batchON op_inventory_ledger(batch_id, transaction_at);CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_ledger_documentON op_inventory_ledger(source_document_type, source_document_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_ledger_warehouseON op_inventory_ledger(warehouse_id, location_id, transaction_at);CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_ledger_typeON op_inventory_ledger(transaction_type, transaction_at);transaction_type values    RAW_MATERIAL_RECEIPTPRODUCTION_ISSUEPRODUCTION_OUTPUTFINISHED_GOODS_RECEIPTWAREHOUSE_TRANSFER_OUTWAREHOUSE_TRANSFER_INSALES_ISSUERETURN_RECEIPTSTOCK_ADJUSTMENT_INSTOCK_ADJUSTMENT_OUTQUARANTINE_MOVE_INQUARANTINE_MOVE_OUTSCRAP_ISSUERECALL_HOLDRECALL_RELEASEPurposeappend-only inventory movement historyphục vụ audit, truy vết, recall, reconciliation8. Inventory Alert RuleCREATE TABLE op_inventory_alert_rule (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    rule_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    rule_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    alert_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,    warehouse_id BIGINT NULL,    days_to_expiry_threshold INT NULL,    qty_threshold NUMERIC(18,3) NULL,    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_inventory_alert_rule_code UNIQUE (rule_code),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_alert_rule_warehouse        FOREIGN KEY (warehouse_id) REFERENCES op_warehouse(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_alert_rule_typeON op_inventory_alert_rule(alert_type, is_active);alert_type valuesNEAR_EXPIRYLOW_STOCKBLOCKED_BATCHQUARANTINE_STOCKRECALL_STOCKPurposerule nền cho dashboard cảnh báo khođặc biệt cho cận date và batch bị khóaX.6 Required Business Semanticsaccepted_qtySố lượng đã được QC accepted từ module QC.warehouse_receipt_qtySố lượng thực tế thủ kho xác nhận nhập kho.variance_qtyPhần chênh lệch giữa:accepted_qtywarehouse_receipt_qtyGiá trị chuẩn:variance_qty = ABS(accepted_qty - warehouse_receipt_qty)Mandatory ruleNếu variance_qty > 0 thì:variance_reason_code bắt buộc cóvariance_note nên bắt buộc ở service layerphải ghi ledger / disposition tương ứng ở bước sauX.7 State Integration RulesBatch state before receiptChỉ batch có trạng thái:    RELEASEDmới được tạo warehouse receipt hợp lệ.Batch state after confirmed receiptSau khi receipt được confirm:    batch_status giữ nguyên RELEASEDvà bắt buộc:· insert ledger FINISHED_GOODS_RECEIPT· update op_inventory_lot_balance· ghi audit log / event log tương ứng cho warehouse receipt· không ghi WAREHOUSE_RECEIVED vào op_batch.batch_statusHard ruleNếu batch_status <> RELEASEDthì phải bị chặn khỏi finished goods receipt. X.8 Quantity Example LockVí dụ chuẩn nghiệp vụ:planned_qty = 2000produced_qty = 2000accepted_qty = 1900warehouse_receipt_qty = 1900variance_qty = 0Ví dụ có chênh lệch:accepted_qty = 1900warehouse_receipt_qty = 1850variance_qty = 5050 còn lại phải được phân loại bằng lý do hợp lệ như:packaging defectQR print errorwrong dateseal openweight mismatchbroken productsensory defecttorn boxwrong 4-sachet ratiopending reworkX.9 Admin Interface RequirementsA. Warehouse DashboardRequired metrics:batches_ready_for_receiptbatches_receivedbatches_on_holdblocked_batchesinventory_by_batchinventory_by_warehouseinventory_by_locationnear_expiry_alertsNguồn dữ liệu:op_batchop_warehouse_receiptop_inventory_lot_balanceop_inventory_alert_ruleB. Receipt ScreenRequired fields:batch_codeaccepted_qtywarehouse_receipt_qtywarehouselocationscanned_batchvariance_warningvariance_reason_codevariance_noteNguồn dữ liệu:op_batchop_batch_quantity_summaryop_warehouseop_warehouse_locationop_warehouse_receiptop_warehouse_receipt_itemC. Inventory Ledger ScreenRequired columns:transaction_timetransaction_typebatchquantitywarehouselocationusersource_documentreasonNguồn dữ liệu:op_inventory_ledgerX.10 Mobile / Warehouse Interface RequirementsWorkflow trên mobile / handheld scanner:open ready-for-receipt batch listscan batchselect warehouseselect locationenter receipt qtyconfirm variance if anysubmit receiptRequired fields:batch_codewarehouse_codelocation_codeaccepted_qtyreceipt_qtyvariance_reason_codeoperator_idreceipt_timestampX.11 Required Service-Layer ControlService: WarehouseReceiptServicePhải thực hiện theo đúng thứ tự:validate batch current state = RELEASEDlấy accepted_qty từ QC / batch quantity summaryvalidate warehouse_receipt_qtynếu lệch, bắt buộc validate reasontạo op_warehouse_receipttạo op_warehouse_receipt_iteminsert op_inventory_ledgerupdate / upsert op_inventory_lot_balanceupdate op_batch_quantity_summary.warehouse_receipt_qtykhông ghi downstream state vào op_batch.batch_statusghi audit / event / source document linkage đúng boundaryService: InventoryLedgerServicePhải chịu trách nhiệm:append inventory movement historyvalidate direction IN / OUTvalidate stock statuskhông cho overwrite ledger row cũForbidden behaviorkhông tăng tồn kho trực tiếp bằng update balance bỏ qua ledgerkhông nhập kho batch chưa RELEASEDkhông bỏ qua variance reason khi số lượng lệchkhông update op_batch.batch_status = WAREHOUSE_RECEIVEDkhông dùng warehouse receipt để chiếm ownership lifecycle của batchX.12 Dev Implementation TasksThứ tự migration đề xuất:061_create_op_warehouse.sql062_create_op_warehouse_location.sql063_create_op_inventory_adjustment_reason.sql064_create_op_warehouse_receipt.sql065_create_op_warehouse_receipt_item.sql066_create_op_inventory_lot_balance.sql067_create_op_inventory_ledger.sql068_create_op_inventory_alert_rule.sqlFolder:/database/operational/05_warehouse_inventory/X.13 Validation TestsTest 1 — Batch must be released before receiptAttempt create warehouse receipt for batch state:QC_PASSQC_HOLDQC_REJECTBLOCKEDExpected result:rejected by service ruleTest 2 — Inventory increases only after confirmed receiptCreate receipt header/item in DRAFT.Expected result:op_inventory_ledger: no RECEIPT row yetop_inventory_lot_balance: no quantity increase yetThen confirm receipt.Expected result:ledger row insertedbalance increasedwarehouse_receipt_qty updatedkhông ghi WAREHOUSE_RECEIVED vào op_batch.batch_statusTest 3 — Variance requires reasonCreate receipt item:accepted_qty = 1900warehouse_receipt_qty = 1850variance_reason_code = NULLExpected result:rejected by service validationTest 4 — Receipt item uniqueness by batch within receiptInsert same batch_id twice in one receipt.Expected result:unique constraint violationTest 5 — Ledger append-only behaviorInsert a receipt ledger row, then need correction.Expected result:create new adjustment rownot overwrite old ledger rowTest 6 — Inventory by batch / warehouse / locationQuery:batch + warehouse + location + stock_statusExpected result:đọc được tồn theo đúng batch, kho, vị tríTest 7 — Near expiry lookupQuery inventory nearing expiry using nearest_exp_date.Expected result:truy vấn nhanh nhờ index phù hợpX.14 Completion CriteriaModule Warehouse Receipt & Inventory Control được xem là khóa xong khi:có warehouse mastercó warehouse location mastercó warehouse receipt header / itemcó adjustment reason referencecó inventory ledger append-onlycó inventory balance by batch / warehouse / locationchỉ batch released mới được nhập khoinventory chỉ tăng sau receipt confirmedvariance bắt buộc có reasonwarehouse receipt confirmed tạo inventory movement và current balance đúng boundary, không ghi downstream state vào op_batch.batch_statusX.15 Technical Lock ResultPhần này khóa xong các nội dung kỹ thuật sau:warehouse master = op_warehousewarehouse location = op_warehouse_locationreceipt transaction = op_warehouse_receipt + op_warehouse_receipt_iteminventory movement history = op_inventory_ledgerinventory current state = op_inventory_lot_balancevariance reason reference = op_inventory_adjustment_reasonalert foundation = op_inventory_alert_ruleKẾT THÚCTRIỂN KHAIXI. STANDARD INVENTORY MODELPhần này khóa mô hình tồn kho chuẩn cho toàn bộ Operational Domain.Inventory phải được quản lý bằng inventory ledger + current balance projection, không cho phép ghi đè số lượng trực tiếp mà không có dấu vết giao dịch.XI.1 Inventory ArchitectureInventory model phải gồm 2 lớp dữ liệu:1. Movement History Layerop_inventory_ledgerChức năng:lưu toàn bộ biến động tồn khoappend-onlyphục vụ auditphục vụ reconciliationphục vụ traceability / recall2. Current Balance Layerop_inventory_lot_balanceChức năng:phản ánh tồn kho hiện tạitối ưu truy vấn nhanh cho:dashboardpickingallocationrecall scopingnear-expiry checkMandatory ruleledger là nguồn lịch sử chuẩnbalance là projection hiện tạikhông được update balance thủ công mà không có ledger entry tương ứngXI.2 Inventory Transaction TypesCác loại giao dịch tồn kho chuẩn phải được khóa thống nhất như sau.1. Raw Material ReceiptNhập nguyên liệu đầu vào.RAW_MATERIAL_RECEIPT2. Production IssueXuất nguyên liệu cho sản xuất.PRODUCTION_ISSUE3. Production OutputGhi nhận sản lượng ra khỏi công đoạn sản xuất.PRODUCTION_OUTPUTTechnical notePRODUCTION_OUTPUT là operational movement, không đồng nghĩa available inventory.Chỉ dùng nếu hệ thống cần theo dõi WIP / finished output trước warehouse receipt.4. Finished Goods ReceiptNhập kho thành phẩm sau QC release.FINISHED_GOODS_RECEIPT5. Warehouse TransferChuyển kho / chuyển vị trí.WAREHOUSE_TRANSFER_OUTWAREHOUSE_TRANSFER_IN6. Sales IssueXuất kho bán hàng / giao đơn hàng.SALES_ISSUE7. Return ReceiptNhận hàng hoàn.RETURN_RECEIPT8. Stock AdjustmentĐiều chỉnh tồn kho.STOCK_ADJUSTMENT_INSTOCK_ADJUSTMENT_OUT9. Quarantine MoveChuyển hàng sang trạng thái cách ly / kho cách ly.QUARANTINE_MOVE_INQUARANTINE_MOVE_OUT10. Scrap IssueXuất hủy / loại bỏ.SCRAP_ISSUEXI.3 Canonical Transaction Type SetĐể tránh mỗi module tự đặt tên khác nhau, khóa bộ transaction type chuẩn cho op_inventory_ledger.transaction_type:RAW_MATERIAL_RECEIPTPRODUCTION_ISSUEPRODUCTION_OUTPUTFINISHED_GOODS_RECEIPTWAREHOUSE_TRANSFER_OUTWAREHOUSE_TRANSFER_INSALES_ISSUERETURN_RECEIPTSTOCK_ADJUSTMENT_INSTOCK_ADJUSTMENT_OUTQUARANTINE_MOVE_INQUARANTINE_MOVE_OUTSCRAP_ISSUERECALL_HOLDRECALL_RELEASEXI.4 Inventory Control RulesRule 1 — No Negative InventoryKhông được xuất âm kho.Required behaviorTrước mọi transaction qty_out, service layer phải kiểm tra:available_qty >= requested_issue_qtyDatabase implicationDB không tự hiểu logic xuất âm theo business context, nên rule này phải khóa ở:service layertransaction procedureallocation validatorAllowed batch state before finished goods receipt    RELEASEDHard ruleNếu batch_status <> RELEASEDthì service phải chặn tạo finished goods receipt.Không liệt kê vocabulary legacy hay downstream state vào op_batch.batch_status.Các trạng thái như:· HOLD· QUARANTINED· BLOCKED· RECALLED· SCRAP· RETURN_PENDING_QCthuộc lớp inventory status / disposition / downstream handling,không phải batch_status canonical của op_batch.Rule 3 — Hold Stock Cannot Enter Selling FlowKhông được đưa hàng hold vào bán hàng.Forbidden stock status for allocation / pickingHOLDQUARANTINEDBLOCKEDRECALLEDSCRAPAllowed stock status for selling flowAVAILABLERule 4 — Returned Goods Must Not Auto-Reenter Good StockHàng hoàn không tự quay lại kho bán tốt nếu chưa QC.Correct flowReturn Receipt      ↓Quarantine / Return Holding      ↓QC / inspection      ↓Disposition      ↓Available OR Scrap OR Rework OR HoldTechnical implicationRETURN_RECEIPT mặc định nên vào:QUARANTINEDhoặcdedicated return locationKhông cho vào AVAILABLE trực tiếp.Rule 5 — Every Adjustment Requires ApprovalMọi điều chỉnh tồn kho phải có:reason codereason noterequested_byapproved_byapproved_atTechnical implicationCác transaction sau phải có approval boundary:STOCK_ADJUSTMENT_INSTOCK_ADJUSTMENT_OUTSCRAP_ISSUEQUARANTINE_MOVE_INQUARANTINE_MOVE_OUTXI.5 Inventory Status ModelĐể các transaction hoạt động nhất quán, tồn kho phải phân loại tối thiểu theo các status sau:ON_HANDAVAILABLEALLOCATEDQUARANTINEDHOLDBLOCKEDDAMAGEDRECALLEDSCRAPRETURN_PENDING_QCStatus meaningON_HANDTồn vật lý đang có trong kho.AVAILABLETồn sẵn sàng cấp cho đơn hàng.ALLOCATEDTồn đã giữ cho đơn hàng.QUARANTINEDTồn bị cách ly chờ xử lý.HOLDTồn bị giữ do quyết định nghiệp vụ / QC / incident.BLOCKEDTồn bị khóa không được cấp phát.DAMAGEDTồn hư hỏng.RECALLEDTồn thuộc phạm vi recall.SCRAPTồn chờ hoặc đã chuyển luồng hủy.RETURN_PENDING_QCHàng hoàn chờ QC.XI.6 Inventory Ledger Semanticsop_inventory_ledger phải tuân theo semantics sau.Mandatory fieldstransaction_typesource_document_typesource_document_idbatch_idwarehouse_idlocation_idstock_statusqty_inqty_outtransaction_atperformed_byDirection ruleMột ledger row chỉ được có:qty_in > 0, qty_out = 0hoặcqty_in = 0, qty_out > 0Không được:đồng thời in và out trên cùng một dòngupdate row cũ để sửa lịch sửXI.7 Recommended Reference Table for Transaction TypesĐể tránh hard-code phân tán, nên bổ sung bảng reference:ref_inventory_transaction_typeCREATE TABLE ref_inventory_transaction_type (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    transaction_type_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    transaction_type_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    direction_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,    affects_available_qty BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,    requires_approval BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    sort_order INT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_ref_inventory_transaction_type_code UNIQUE (transaction_type_code),    CONSTRAINT ck_ref_inventory_transaction_type_direction        CHECK (direction_type IN ('IN', 'OUT', 'BOTH', 'STATUS_ONLY')));CREATE INDEX idx_ref_inventory_transaction_type_activeON ref_inventory_transaction_type(is_active, sort_order);Purposechuẩn hóa loại giao dịch tồn khophục vụ validation service layerphục vụ dashboard / reporting / auditExample seedRAW_MATERIAL_RECEIPT | IN   | false | falsePRODUCTION_ISSUE     | OUT  | false | falsePRODUCTION_OUTPUT    | IN   | false | falseFINISHED_GOODS_RECEIPT | IN | true  | falseWAREHOUSE_TRANSFER_OUT | OUT | false | falseWAREHOUSE_TRANSFER_IN  | IN  | false | falseSALES_ISSUE          | OUT  | true  | falseRETURN_RECEIPT       | IN   | false | falseSTOCK_ADJUSTMENT_IN  | IN   | true  | trueSTOCK_ADJUSTMENT_OUT | OUT  | true  | trueQUARANTINE_MOVE_IN   | BOTH | false | trueQUARANTINE_MOVE_OUT  | BOTH | false | trueSCRAP_ISSUE          | OUT  | false | trueRECALL_HOLD          | STATUS_ONLY | false | trueRECALL_RELEASE       | STATUS_ONLY | false | trueXI.8 Required Approval Model for AdjustmentsNên bổ sung transaction approval object cho các adjustment nhạy cảm.op_inventory_adjustment_approvalCREATE TABLE op_inventory_adjustment_approval (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    approval_no VARCHAR(120) NOT NULL,    transaction_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    source_document_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    source_document_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    warehouse_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    requested_qty NUMERIC(18,3) NOT NULL,    reason_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    reason_note TEXT NULL,    requested_by BIGINT NOT NULL,    requested_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,    approval_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'PENDING',    approved_by BIGINT NULL,    approved_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    rejected_by BIGINT NULL,    rejected_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    decision_note TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_inventory_adjustment_approval_no UNIQUE (approval_no),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_adjustment_approval_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_adjustment_approval_warehouse        FOREIGN KEY (warehouse_id) REFERENCES op_warehouse(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_inventory_adjustment_approval_reason        FOREIGN KEY (reason_code) REFERENCES op_inventory_adjustment_reason(reason_code),    CONSTRAINT ck_op_inventory_adjustment_approval_qty        CHECK (requested_qty > 0));CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_adjustment_approval_statusON op_inventory_adjustment_approval(approval_status, requested_at);CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_adjustment_approval_batchON op_inventory_adjustment_approval(batch_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_inventory_adjustment_approval_typeON op_inventory_adjustment_approval(transaction_type);approval_status valuesPENDINGAPPROVEDREJECTEDCANCELLEDPurposephê duyệt điều chỉnh tồn khokhóa rule “mọi điều chỉnh phải có phê duyệt”XI.9 Required Service-Layer RulesInventoryLedgerServicePhải chịu trách nhiệm:tạo ledger entriesvalidate transaction typevalidate directionvalidate batch state / stock statusvalidate no-negative-inventorycập nhật balance projectionInventoryAdjustmentServicePhải chịu trách nhiệm:tạo request điều chỉnhkiểm tra reason codekiểm tra quyền phê duyệtchỉ sau APPROVED mới được tạo ledger adjustmentAllocationGuardServicePhải chặn allocation nếu:batch chưa released / warehouse_received hợp lệstock_status không phải AVAILABLEavailable_qty không đủXI.10 Validation Rules by Transaction TypeRAW_MATERIAL_RECEIPTcho phép tăng tồn nguyên liệukhông liên quan available finished goodsPRODUCTION_ISSUEchỉ được xuất nếu raw material stock đủkhông âm kho nguyên liệuPRODUCTION_OUTPUTkhông tự động vào available inventoryFINISHED_GOODS_RECEIPTbatch phải RELEASEDreceipt phải confirmedtạo ledger INcập nhật balanceSALES_ISSUEbatch phải thuộc stock AVAILABLEkhông âm khotạo forward trace linkRETURN_RECEIPTkhông vào available trực tiếpmặc định vào RETURN_PENDING_QC hoặc QUARANTINEDSTOCK_ADJUSTMENT_IN / OUTbắt buộc approvalbắt buộc reasonQUARANTINE_MOVE_IN / OUTbắt buộc approval hoặc incident/QC trigger hợp lệSCRAP_ISSUEbắt buộc approvalbắt buộc reasonphải giảm tồn đúng batchXI.11 Dashboard / UI ImplicationsWarehouse dashboard phải đọc được:tồn theo batchtồn theo trạng tháitồn theo kho / vị trístock on holdstock quarantinedstock recallednear expiryLedger screen phải đọc được:transaction typebatchqty in/outwarehouselocationactorsource documentreasonapproval status nếu cóXI.12 Dev Implementation TasksNếu tiếp tục khóa phần inventory model này ở mức schema, bổ sung 2 migration:069_create_ref_inventory_transaction_type.sql070_create_op_inventory_adjustment_approval.sqlFolder:/database/operational/05_warehouse_inventory/XI.13 Validation TestsTest 1 — No negative inventoryGiả sử available_qty = 100.Attempt:SALES_ISSUE = 120Expected result:bị chặn ở service validationTest 2 — Return receipt cannot auto-availableCreate RETURN_RECEIPT.Expected result:stock status mặc định là RETURN_PENDING_QC hoặc QUARANTINEDkhông tăng AVAILABLETest 3 — Adjustment requires approvalCreate STOCK_ADJUSTMENT_OUT without approval.Expected result:không được insert ledger chính thứcTest 4 — Hold stock excluded from salesAttempt allocate batch in status:HOLDQUARANTINEDRECALLEDExpected result:bị loại khỏi allocation candidate setTest 5 — Production output not equal available inventoryCreate PRODUCTION_OUTPUT.Expected result:không tạo stock AVAILABLEchỉ khi FINISHED_GOODS_RECEIPT confirmed mới tăng available inventoryXI.14 Completion CriteriaPhần Standard Inventory Model được xem là khóa xong khi:inventory dùng ledger + balance projectiontransaction types được chuẩn hóakhông có âm khokhông có finished goods receipt trước QC releasehold stock không vào bán hànghàng hoàn không quay lại good stock nếu chưa QCmọi điều chỉnh tồn kho có approval objectXI.15 Technical Lock ResultPhần này khóa xong các nội dung kỹ thuật sau:inventory model = ledger-driventransaction taxonomy = standardizedno negative inventory = mandatory validationno pre-release finished goods receiptno hold stock sellingno auto-good return stockadjustment approval = mandatory control layerKẾT THÚCTRIỂN KHAIXII. TRACEABILITY & BATCH GENEALOGY ENGINE – DATABASE SCHEMAModule này triển khai truy xuất 2 chiều, genealogy nội bộ, public trace page và impact trace phục vụ incident / recall.Đây là module nối toàn bộ chuỗi:raw materialproductionpackagingQCwarehouseallocationshipmentcustomer exposureXII.1 Functional ObjectiveModule phải đáp ứng đồng thời 3 nhóm truy vấn:1. Forward TraceTừ:raw material lot→ production order→ finished batch→ warehouse→ shipment allocation→ shipment link→ customer exposure2. Backward TraceTừ:batchQR tokenshipmentorderquay ngược về:raw material lotproduction orderproduction stepline / machine / operatorQCwarehouse receipt3. Impact TraceTừ:defective batchincident casexác định:còn tồn ở kho nàođã phân bổ cho shipment nàođã đi đến customer exposure nàocó cần recall hay khôngXII.2 Core Design RulesRule 1 — Genealogy must be key-basedMọi liên kết genealogy phải dựa trên khóa dữ liệu chuẩn:raw_material_lot_idproduction_order_idexecution_idbatch_idpackaging_job_unit_idqc_inspection_idwarehouse_receipt_idshipment_idcustomer_idKhông dùng text note làm khóa nối.Rule 2 — Internal genealogy and public trace must be separatedPublic trace page chỉ đọc projection công khai.Không đọc trực tiếp toàn bộ genealogy nội bộ.Rule 3 — Every finished batch must support minimum backward traceMọi batch thành phẩm phải truy ngược được ít nhất đến:raw material lotproduction orderQC inspectionwarehouse receiptRule 4 — Every sold batch must support minimum forward traceMọi batch đã bán phải truy xuôi được ít nhất đến:shipment allocationshipment linkcustomer exposureRule 5 — Recall must reuse genealogy dataRecall Engine phải dùng trực tiếp dữ liệu genealogy / traceability / exposure chain,không dựng logic truy xuất riêng.Rule 6 — Bridge tables do not replace source of truthCác bảng bridge/query-optimized chỉ phục vụ:traceabilityimpact analysisrecall executionkhông thay thế source of truth nghiệp vụ gốc ở:batchwarehouse receiptinventory ledgershipment allocationXII.3 Core EntitiesModule này tạo / sử dụng các bảng chính sau:A. Bảng cục bộ của moduleop_production_stepop_trace_qr_registryop_trace_search_indexop_incident_history_linkop_shipment_batch_linkop_customer_batch_exposureop_recall_customer_linkop_batch_genealogy_linkB. Bảng nguồn genealogy / traceability từ các phase trướcop_raw_material_lotop_production_orderop_production_executionop_batchop_qc_inspectionop_warehouse_receiptop_warehouse_receipt_itemop_inventory_ledgerop_inventory_lot_balanceop_batch_material_usageop_batch_releaseop_shipment_allocationXII.4 Database Schema1. Source Zone Reuse RuleModule Traceability không tạo bảng source zone mới.Bảng canonical của source zone đã được tạo ở module Growing Zone / Source Origin Traceability:Rule cứng:· Traceability Engine chỉ đọc lại ref_source_zone· không dùng free-text source_region làm khóa join canonical· source_region trong op_raw_material_receipt chỉ là display snapshot tương thích ngượcCanonical join:op_raw_material_receipt.source_zone_id→ ref_source_zone.id2. Production StepCREATE TABLE op_production_step (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    execution_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    batch_id BIGINT NULL,    step_code VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,    step_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    step_sequence INT NOT NULL,    machine_id BIGINT NULL,    operator_id BIGINT NULL,    started_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    completed_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    step_status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'COMPLETED',    note TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    created_by BIGINT NULL,    updated_by BIGINT NULL,    is_deleted BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,    deleted_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    CONSTRAINT fk_op_production_step_execution        FOREIGN KEY (execution_id) REFERENCES op_production_execution(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_production_step_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_production_step_machine        FOREIGN KEY (machine_id) REFERENCES op_machine(id),    CONSTRAINT uq_op_production_step_unique        UNIQUE (execution_id, step_sequence, step_code));CREATE INDEX idx_op_production_step_batchON op_production_step(batch_id, step_sequence);CREATE INDEX idx_op_production_step_executionON op_production_step(execution_id, step_sequence);Purposechuẩn hóa công đoạn để render genealogy tree / timelinekhông suy luận từ event text rời rạc3. Trace QR RegistryCREATE TABLE op_trace_qr_registry (    id BIGINT GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY PRIMARY KEY,    qr_token VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,    qr_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'BOX',    batch_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    packaging_job_unit_id BIGINT NULL,    sku_id BIGINT NOT NULL,    public_trace_url TEXT NOT NULL,    issued_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,    invalidated_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    invalidation_reason TEXT NULL,    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,    created_by BIGINT NULL,    updated_by BIGINT NULL,    is_deleted BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,    deleted_at TIMESTAMP NULL,    CONSTRAINT uq_op_trace_qr_registry_token UNIQUE (qr_token),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_trace_qr_registry_batch        FOREIGN KEY (batch_id) REFERENCES op_batch(id),    CONSTRAINT fk_op_trace_qr_registry_packaging_unit        FOREIGN KEY (packaging_job_unit_id) REFERENCES op_packaging_job_unit(id));CREATE INDEX idx_op_trace_qr_registry_batchON op_trace_qr_registry(batch_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_trace_qr_registry_packaging_unitON op_trace_qr_registry(packaging_job_unit_id);CREATE INDEX idx_op_trace_qr_registry_activeON op_trace_qr_registry(is_active, issued_at);qr_type valuesBOXSACHETBATCHPurposeregistry token QR để tra cứu public trace / internal tracekhông để public page quét trực tiếp toàn bộ nội bộ4.
